<Date>1591293815993< /Date><Rating>5< /Rating>< text>
State of the art storage. Everything about Trojan is 10x better than other storage facilities.

Applaud the owner and operations. Seriously great deals better facilities than anything you'll find.

Incredible front office service Lachelle and the other front desk person (handsome australian man sorry didnt want to get your name wrong) are seriously perfect. Professional, polite, even headed, customer friendly and while I don't recommend doing this, I had temporarily misplaced keys, had movers come to liquidate my design furnishings and drop off items 2x and due to their tight timeline, 2nd time they couldn't wait to have items stored. Lachelle went above and beyond to make sure my items were secure until I could get them into my storage. That is going way above and beyond.

I purchased 10 queen and king size mattress bags which worked great for all the mattress I was storing for staging.

They have great prices on their protective materials and merchandise. It's well worth the $5 to protect a $1000+ mattress set and it fit the king size mattress and boxspring.

The 2 storage 10x10s I rented were immaculate the facility is very very well run, great ac, no dust literally AT ALL, no moisture and I can't have it as humidity ruins furnishings. Well lit, safe, the security codes they have you create for each storage garage controls both the front gate and access to the elevator and keys your smart garage know you're on your way there to access your garage.

I am a super happy customer. Not paid to do this review!!! Just relieved I found you guys when I really needed it and it feels really clean and safe.  Also not crowded though it has the capacity. Smart use of space for lockers that you can keep files in though I needed more space for furnishings.< /text>

<Text>When the local Home Depots ran our of hay I turned to Damoor's for my Halloween decorative needs.

Damoor's serves the equestrian community in Burbank and as such has plenty of hay (straw) year-round.

It turned out that the bales were cheaper here than at Home Depot; about $2 less at $11 per bale.

I also learned that they will not take the unused straw for health reasons even if you just want to give it back.  Inquire with the stables in the area to see who will take it once you tear down your Halloween set-up.

#ReviewItForward</Text><Pictures>None< /Pictures><resp>None<//resp>< gmapID>

<rating>5</rating>< Time>
1598230573048</Time>
<text>I was exposed to someone who tested positive for COVID-19, and I had my COVID-19 test taken here, and opted for the rapid testing, with results within 30 minutes due to my need to return to my family. You need to at least have 4-5 days from exposure to test time.

So my review is only in relation to the COVID-19 rapid testing. The process is quick, the staff is friendly and courteous.

You MUST set an appointment online.

Check in at your appointment time, you will need your ID. You will fill out some quick forms, provide your phone number, then pay. You will then return to your car and await their phone call. It's best to move and park upfront so they can better locate you, they will be swabbing your nasal cavity in your car.

Afterwards, it takes about 30 minutes and they will come out to your car to deliver your results.

Good luck!<//text>< resp>
None</resp>

< Text>
TERRBILE EXPERIENCE. We had probably the worst experience at healthcare facility with this Urgent Care office. My mother fractured 1 of her fingers from a door slamming into it. We came to the office by their recommendation so they could take some xrays. The PA confirmed the fracture and suggested we see an ortho within a week, and we should pick up her xrays in a few days. We scheduled an ortho visit a week after, and we came back to the urgent care office to get the xrays. After waiting for almost 25 minutes, the receptionist, who had a scowl on her face the entire time, gave us a piece of paper that says the radiologist confirms the fracture. We needed the actual XRAY SCANS for the ortho to look at, NOT a radiology report. We asked the receptionist for the scans and waited another 15 minutes, only for someone to tell us that they do not have the physical scans, and the "xray guy" just left the building. We had the ortho appointment in 30 minutes, and at this point I was furious. After an intense argument with a PA or nurse (i'm not sure), they finally gave me a LINK to the digital xray scans. Why did they not give us this in the first place?? Why did I need to argue loudly with a nurse to get our xray scans (that we paid out of pocket for as well)??
Fast forward a month (July 22) , my mother decided to go to another ortho office, and we tried accessing the LINK given by Xpress urgent care, but it has EXPIRED 4 days after it was given to me. Once again, we went to the office to get the link and waited for 30 minutes, only to hear that no one there could provide the link again and the "xray guy" is out of the building... AGAIN. They said they would try to contact the main office in Tustin to figure this out. 15 minutes later, we would told there was NOTHING they could do. NOTHING. They told us to go on to our ortho appointment and they'll send the link when they figure it out. We honestly lost all hope at this point and left with no xray scans for our ortho. He was not happy because he needed the records to see how my mother's finger has healed. We finally received that link 3 hours later. At which point, we already finished the visit with our ortho. I normally never write reviews, let alone bad reviews. But our experience with this office was so incredibly stressful, dissapointing and frustrating that I had to.<//Text>
